	<script>
// Adjust the number values below to match the height of the content above
window.onscroll = function() {scrollFunction()};
 
function scrollFunction() {
  if (document.body.scrollTop > 50 || document.documentElement.scrollTop > 50) {
    document.getElementById("main-top-menu-custom").style.position = "fixed"; 
    document.getElementById("main-top-menu-custom").style.width = "100%";
    document.getElementById("header-row-custom").classList.add('MyClass');
    
  } else {
    document.getElementById("main-top-menu-custom").style.position = "";
    document.getElementById("main-top-menu-custom").style.width = "100%";
    document.getElementById("header-row-custom").classList.remove('MyClass');
  }
}
</script>
